<Review>Dr. Morshedi, John, & Catherine all do a great job of making everyone feel welcome while also giving some of the best dental care I've ever received.
Catherine is always a step ahead of any insurance issues and makes every phone call or step in the door feel like you're interacting with family. With Catherine doing as much work on the paperwork side in advance and the efficient working relationship between Dr. Morshedi & John, I'm often in-and-out in 30 minutes for a cleaning.
Make no mistake, though, I've never felt rushed. After a warm welcome from Catherine, she or John start the visit off with a warm and scented neck pillow. The little niceties keep coming through the procedure itself with glasses to help block the bright light of the overhead lamp.
If they have to do any drilling, they offer a radio and headphones to help block that shrilling noise. I found even more comfort in realizing how up to date Dr. Morshedi stays on dental technologies. It sucks to have to get a filling re-done, but, dang it, it was so cool to see her take a 3D image of my mouth and then walk right down the hall to get my new filling off her printer.
Finally, whether it is a standard cleaning or another procedure, the cherry, er, maybe lavender on top, is a fresh lavender-scented towel to wipe off your face. After a quick stop with Catherine to schedule your next appointment, you're out the door feeling calmer than when you stepped through it.< /Review><pics>None< /pics>< resp>

<review>We had a nice dinner there last night with the Soup is the Day, Chicken Taco Appetizer, Seasonal Salad Special and the Beyond Burger with Sweet Potato Fries! The beer and Ale menu continues to impress.
The service was much better than our last visit 3 weeks ago.
Looks like the Beyond Meat Burger, which could be substituted for any of the burgers on their menu is there to stay!
We found a decent food menu and excellent variety of ales, beers (30) and Kombucha (2).

<response>None</response><name>Jennifer Rich</name>< Review>
Had the lamb burger a year ago and it was great. Ordered it tonight for delivery and it was terrible. And not because of the delivery: the bun was about 5 inches across, the patty... about 3 inches across and less than half an inch thick. V. dry though the flavor was good enough and a bit spicy. The bun was soggy and falling apart in the very middle while the outside was hard and dry as if it were stale (with absolutely no filling in the dry parts as the meat portion was so small). The "dressing" for the burger was a small splotch in the very center of the already tiny and sad patty. Dont know if it was an off night, but so disappointing I won't be trying their food again... especially at $15 for that sad sad lamb burger!<//Review>

Here I am on a chilly Thursday evening inside one of Albany's charming establishments: The Albany Taproom. Service was slow. I came in alone after work and the staff is more concerned with interacting with each other than interacting with guests. Their loss!

Onto the beer folks! 32 selections and I choose the barley wine from Napa Smith. 10 ounces, 10% carmel notes, toffee aftertaste, not too heavy on the palate. It's a winner. Atmosphere is nice. Place is busy. Plenary of seating. I chose to not order food.

Great selection of beer. Good service when they get to you. Knowledgeable staff. Decently priced. Surprising bottle selection.

Atmosphere 4/5
Service 4/5
Beer 5/5< /text>

<date>1469053762673</date><Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
The Taproom and Grazzy Burgers next door go hand in hand.  The rooms are interjoining, and whichever entrance you use, you can order beer from the Taproom and food from Grazzy Burgers. If you like a brighter restaurant-type environment then sit on the Grazzy Burgers side, or if you prefer a darker pub atmosphere then sit on the Taproom side.  I‚Äôve been here about half a dozen times (sitting in the Taproom side each time) and have always found the service to be super-helpful and the food to arrive promptly and exactly as ordered. To those that quibble about the prices being a little high, I would disagree - $9 (or even $11) for a burger is not a high price when you consider that the meat is humanely raised, grass-fed, locally sourced, and served on an organic Acme bun‚Ä¶ and delicious.

Beer: Check the Taproom website for a picture of their chalkboard listing the 32 or so beers that they have on tap. Mostly local ‚Äìyou‚Äôll see some familiar names (Fieldwork, Henhouse, North Coast, Stone, Drake‚Äôs, Altamont) but also some very unfamiliar brews, even from breweries that you know fairly well.  A recent highlight for me was North Coast‚Äôs Old Stock Ale, aged in rye whiskey barrels (its brother aged in wheat whiskey barrels was also available). It‚Äôs a dark ale, almost 14% alcohol ($8 for 10 oz) but yet isn‚Äôt overpowered by the ethanol or the whiskey flavors ‚Äì it was well-balanced, potent, and very, very good. Another good one was Drake‚Äôs Unholy Alliance sour ale, fermented with Viognier grape skins from Rockwall cellars (also $8 for 10 oz). Yep, beer is getting pretty fancy these days and the Taproom is a good place to find out what‚Äôs new ‚Äì and you can also get pints of well-made traditional beers and ales for $5-6. The friendly bartenders were happy to pour samples and frequently checked our table for orders.

Sustainability: I‚Äôm also giving the Taproom and Grazzy Burgers experience 5/5 green stars for social and environmental impact. Green stars you say? Why yes! It‚Äôs a new rating scale for social and environmental impact - it‚Äôll catch on ;) The Taproom‚Äôs beer is predominantly from very local breweries and many of these (Drake‚Äôs, North Coast, Stone, to name a few) are making good efforts on energy use, re-use of spent grains, and philanthropic causes. Grazzy Burgers use mostly organic ingredients, all sourced from Bay Area farms, and again, those excellent organic buns are from Acme. Their meat is grass-fed (corn-free), compassionately raised without stress or confinement, antibiotics, or hormones and their salmon is wild. The pasture-raised beef and lamb comes from employee-owned Sun-Fed Ranch and Superior Farms (the latter is also 50% wind-powered).

The food: I‚Äôve had their black bean fiesta burger, sweet potato fries, Kennebec fries, regular fries, onion rings, and hummus plate. My favorite is the black bean burger ($9), which comes with a side of homemade potato chips (fries is $2 extra). There were maybe four things that stood out: first, it was a real, homemade burger and not a super-dense soy protein or gluten patty and it was satisfyingly filling without being overly heavy. Second, it had this lemony flavor, not over-lemony but providing just enough acid, that really elevated it. I checked the menu and this delicious flavor was coming from the preserved lemon guacamole. Third, it was moist and had enough toppings (the guacamole, pico de gallo, and cilantro lime aioli) that I wasn‚Äôt even remotely tempted to reach for ketchup or mustard. Fourth ‚Äì the bun was great. So many otherwise great burgers are let down by their buns ‚Äì story of my life really. My friend had the Grazzy Classic beef burger (also $9) and like it a lot too ‚Äì good bun and cooked to order.</Review>

I have been her more than a couple of times and have to say it's a great little spot. Sometimes the service isn't the fastest or most attentive but the servers and bartenders are hella nice. The food is great and not your basic pub fare. Everything's got a little twist to it, like harrisa ketchup, they've got sweet potato fries and "dino" chips aka kale chips. The beet salad (plus chicken if it strikes your fancy) is pretty stellar. Overall the food tastes fresh and is full of good ingredients. It's hard to go wrong with such a wonderfully vast rotating beer selection and cooler! Definitely a happy camper when I leave!< /Review>

<UserId.>103315700015915152757</UserId.><name>Anthony Brooks< /name>< time>
1558222525021</time>
<Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
This is a cool little quiet park hidden behind a business park. It was a great spot to get away from from pretty much everyone as there was no one here at all. The park is well kept up, has picnic tables and well maintained trails. At the front there is also a trail connected to it that goes for quite aways back with some cool different plants and trees. There are signs that tell you the different trees and shrubs along the way. I would recommend this spot for a family picnic or to get away from people.<//Text>

<Rate>5</Rate><Review>Moving here has been an absolute dream. Everything in the apartment from the floors to the ceilings are so well made. I really don't consider this an apartment complex. It feels more like a condo/townhouse.

The noticeable difference here is how quiet it is! I was not used to this at all. (We do live at the very back of the complex and don't face any other units, which is probably why it is so quiet.)

One of our top reasons why we love living here is because of all the things we can do in walking distance. We are able to walk to Trader Joe's (takes 3 minutes), walk to Chumash Park (maybe 2 minute walk), and we've even walked to the Starbucks on Kanan from the park.

We have gone in the pool 3 times in the last week (in the afternoon and in the evening) and nobody was in the pool. Felt so private! The pool is also extremely clean and way bigger than I remembered.

Since our balcony is facing the back of the complex, we do have a view of a warehouse. But it doesn't bother us much since they are only open during the week while we are at work anyways.

The one thing (the fact that there is literally only one thing is amazing) that I wish they had was a spray nozzle for the kitchen sink. It doesn't have the faucet extender so it is a little difficult to spray down big pots in the sink.

Another HUGE plus to this place, ceiling fans! On the lowest level you can't even hear the fan. So we sleep with it on all night.

But probably hands down, one of the #1 reasons why we love living here is the parking. You get 2 assigned parking spots in the underground garage. You have a remote that opens the gate and a key that opens a door on the side of the garage. It's super safe and secure. And then any above ground parking is free to whoever. Not having the stress of no parking (like your average apartment complex) is a huge relief. Yes, this apartment is more on the pricier side, but I'm telling you every penny is worth it. The extra hundred dollars you pay a month is paying for privacy, parking, landscape, the pool, the gym (which is amazing), peaceful surroundings, distance to everything, hiking trails, high quality hardware, large living spaces, speedy maintenance response, super friendly staff, etc.

Also, they have food trucks every month that come and park at the complex!
